Then she informed me that there was a room that was being cleaned and it would take 40 minutes. I came to ask for the third time at around 3 o'clock, and the front desk called one by one to ask about the rooms. I really find it strange. Is there any hotel that requires you to call the cleaning aunt one by one to see if there are any rooms, and then tell me that there are none? I came again and again with the elderly and children, and finally alarmed the leader, who said to go up and see if there are any rooms that have been cleaned. When I went up, I saw that there was a room that had been cleaned for us to check in. msg:Zhanjiang Garden Hotel enjoys a unique geographical location. The guest room is large, with plenty of space for the cloakroom, dressing table, and double vanity. The bathroom is separated from wet and dry, and the bathtub is large and close to the window, so you can watch the sea and take a bath without missing a beat. Through the floor-to-ceiling windows of the room, you can enjoy the invincible sea view and experience the quality experience of resting on the sea and listening to the waves. Out of the hotel gate is the blue sea and coconut grove, the beach and blue sky, and the sea view is simply yyds. The landmark of Zhanjiang lying on the sea - the Bay Bridge can be seen clearly. There are two Shopping Malls around, so it is very convenient to eat, shop and go shopping. On the left of the hotel is the Jinshawan Shopping Center, and on the right is the Cosmopolitan Shopping Center. The hotel service is very good. I received a call asking if I had any special needs before I checked in. The first impression was very good. The cleaners on the 39th floor were polite and attentive. When they saw that I was hanging up the washed clothes in the room, they took the initiative to use a vertical mobile drying rack with towels spread underneath, which really warmed my heart. The freshly made handmade fine noodles for breakfast is the signature and tastes good. The female chef is fast and polite, and the service attitude is very good. It feels good to stay for 3 nights, and I will still choose Garden Hotel when I come to Zhanjiang in the future.
